Three men have been found sat on the rudder of a ship after an 11-day journey. The ship had arrived in Las Palmas, Gran Canaria, from Nigeria's largest city Lagos - a journey of more than 2,700 nautical miles - according to data from maritime tracking sites. A photo shared by the Spanish coastguard shows their feet less than a metre above the water, as they sit on the rudder at the oil tanker's stern. The men were taken to hospital at the tanker's destination in Gran Canaria and treated for moderate dehydration. Tap the link in our bio to find out about similar incidents. Beefy Bums recovery day🥵🥶 Just a little paradise right in my backyard going from 155 degrees in my @sunhomesaunas to @the.coldplunge at 50 degrees. I haven’t always loved extreme heat, but it always feels damn good getting in the sauna. It helps make stretching easier, relieves my tension headaches, and is a great way to detox. Cold I also haven’t always loved, but I have definitely learned to love ice baths as they help me reduce overall inflammation which is great for my autoimmune and overall health. Used alone they’re both awesome, but together their benefits just stack on top of each other, such as helping circulation/blood flow leading to greater heart health, reducing stress in the body, muscle recovery, and more. Trying to keep this body running like a damn machine for as long as possible.🤖 @sunhomesaunas @the.coldplunge
